[29/10/23, 5:25:30â€¯PM] Abdul Shaikh: # Tic Tac Toe board represented as a list of lists
board = [[' ', ' ', ' '],
         [' ', ' ', ' '],
         [' ', ' ', ' ']]

# Function to print the Tic Tac Toe board
def print_board(board):
    for row in board:
        print('|'.join(row))
        print('-' * 5)

# Function to check if a player has won
def check_winner(board, player):
    # Check rows
    for row in board:
        if row[0] == row[1] == row[2] == player:
            return True

    # Check columns
    for col in range(3):
        if board[0][col] == board[1][col] == board[2][col] == player:
            return True

    # Check diagonals
    if (board[0][0] == board[1][1] == board[2][2] == player) or (board[0][2] == board[1][1] == board[2][0] == player):
        return True

    return False



# Function to check if the board is full
def is_board_full(board):
    for row in board:
        if ' ' in row:
            return False
    return True

# Main game loop
def play_game():
    current_player = 'X'
    while True:
        print_board(board)

        if current_player == 'X':
            row, col = map(int, input("Enter your move (row[0-2] column[0-2]): ").split())
            if board[row][col] != ' ':
                print("Invalid move, try again.")
                continue
            board[row][col] = 'X'
        else:
            row, col = map(int, input("Enter your move (row[0-2] column[0-2]): ").split())
            if board[row][col] != ' ':
                print("Invalid move, try again.")
                continue
            board[row][col] = 'O'


        if check_winner(board, current_player):
            print_board(board)
            print(f"{current_player} wins!")
            break

        elif is_board_full(board):
            print_board(board)
            print("It's a draw!")
            break

        current_player = 'O' if current_player == 'X' else 'X'

# Start the game
play_game()

[01/11/23, 9:05:05â€¯PM] Abdul Shaikh: @WebMethod(operationName = "caesar")
    public String caesar(@WebParam(name = "text") String text, @WebParam(name = "key") int key) {
        
        String encrypted = "";
        
        for( int i = 0 ; i < text.length(); i++ ){
            encrypted += (char)(text.charAt(i) + key);
        }
        return encrypted;
    }
    
       @WebMethod(operationName = "caesar_decrypt")
    public String caesar_decrypt(@WebParam(name = "ciphertext") String ciphertext, @WebParam(name = "key") int key) {
        
        String decrypted = "";
        
        for( int i = 0 ; i < ciphertext.length(); i++ ){
            decrypted += (char)(ciphertext.charAt(i) - key);
        }
        return decrypted;
    }

[02/11/23, 10:24:04â€¯AM] Abdul Shaikh: @WebMethod(operationName = "enc")
    public String enc(@WebParam(name = "message") String message, @WebParam(name = "key") String key){
        
        try{
        //TODO write your implementation code here:
        SecretKeySpec deskey = new SecretKeySpec(key.getBytes(),"DES") ;
        Cipher cipher = Cipher.getInstance("DES");
        cipher.init(Cipher.ENCRYPT_MODE, deskey);
        byte[] encrypt = cipher.doFinal(message.getBytes());
        
        String encrypted_msg = Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(encrypt);
                
        
        return encrypted_msg;
        }
        
        catch (Exception e){
            return e.toString();
        }
    }

    /**
     * Web service operation
     */
    @WebMethod(operationName = "dec")
    public String dec(@WebParam(name = "message") String message, @WebParam(name = "key") String key) throws NoSuchAlgorithmException, NoSuchPaddingException, InvalidKeyException, IllegalBlockSizeException, BadPaddingException {
        //TODO write your implementation code here:
        
        SecretKeySpec deskey = new SecretKeySpec(key.getBytes(), "DES");
        Cipher cipher = Cipher.getInstance("DES");
        cipher.init(Cipher.DECRYPT_MODE, deskey);
        
        byte [] encrypted_msg = Base64.getDecoder().decode(message);
        
        byte [] decrypt =  cipher.doFinal(encrypted_msg);
        
        String decrypted_msg = new String(decrypt);
        
        return decrypted_msg;
    }

            <tr>
                <th>Id</th>
                <th>Name</th>
            </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody id="data"></tbody>
        </table>
        <script>
            window.onload = async () => {
                const response = await fetch("REST RESOURCE URI LINK HERE");
                const text = await response.text();
                const xml = new DOMParser().parseFromString(text, "text/xml");
                const elements = xml.getElementsByTagName("namedetails");
                let data = "";
                for (let i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
                    const name = elements[i].getElementsByTagName("name")[0].childNodes[0].nodeValue;
                    const id = elements[i].getElementsByTagName("id")[0].childNodes[0].nodeValue;
                    data += `<tr><td>${id}</td><td>${name}</td></tr>`;
                }
                document.getElementById("data").innerHTML = data;
            }
        </script>
    </body>
</html>

# next create a socket object

# we have not typed any ip in the ip field
# instead we have inputted an empty string
# this makes the server listen to requests
# coming from other computers on the network

rank_val={"A":1,"B":1,"C":1,"D":1}

def find_inward_edges(stri):
    inward=[]
    for i in vector_dict:
        if stri in vector_dict[i]:
            inward.append(i)
    return inward


def outDegree(edge):
    for i in edge:
        return(len(vector_dict[i]))

edges_pt = find_inward_edges("D")


print("Edges are: ",edges_pt)
print("",outDegree(edges_pt))

rank_a=1

#[ for i in range(5)]
def find_incom(stri):
    incom=[]
    for i in vector_dict:
        if stri in vector_dict[i]:
            incom.append(i)
    return incom
print(find_incom("C"))
 

def calc_pagerank(vector_dict):
    df=0.85
    for i in range(3):
        for j in vector_dict:
            incom=find_incom(j)
            pagerank=(1-df)+df*sum([rank_val[z]/len(vector_dict[z]) for z in incom])
            rank_val[j] = pagerank
 
calc_pagerank(vector_dict)
print(rank_val)

[16/01/24, 11:31:14â€¯PM] ~Mahek Mulani: Description

Chi-squared test, a statistical method, is used by machine learning methods to check the correlation between two categorical variables.

Chi-Square distribution

A random variable ê­“ follows chi-square distribution if it can be written as a sum of squared standard normal variables.



Degrees of freedom

Degrees of freedom refers to the maximum number of logically independent values, which have the freedom to vary.


A chi-square test is used in statistics to test the independence of two events. Given the data of two variables, we can get observed count O and expected count E. Chi-Square measures how expected count E and observed count O deviates each other.



Steps to perform the Chi-Square Test
â— Define Hypothesis.
â— Build a Contingency table.
â— Find the expected values.
â— Calculate the Chi-Square statistic.
â— Accept or Reject the Null Hypothesis.



Role/Importance
The Chi-square test is intended to test how likely it is that an observed distribution is due to chance. It is also called a â€œgoodness of fitâ€ statistic,because it measures how well the observed distribution of data fits with the distribution that is expected if the variables are independent.

A Chi-square test is designed to analyze categorical data. That means that the
data has been counted and divided into categories.

5% level of significance â€“ prob of rejecting null hypothesis when it is true

[30/03/24, 1:13:25â€¯AM] Abdul Shaikh: Q34. When Case law can be implemented? (REPEATED)
Ans: Case law, also known as precedent or common law, refers to the body of legal decisions and interpretations made by courts in previous cases. Case law can be implemented or applied in several ways within the legal system:

1. **Interpretation of Laws**:
   - Case law plays a crucial role in interpreting statutes, regulations, and other legal provisions.
   - Courts may rely on precedents established in previous cases to interpret the meaning and application of laws in similar or related circumstances.

2. **Establishing Legal Precedent**:
   - Court decisions create legal precedents that serve as authoritative interpretations of the law.
   - Once a court establishes a precedent in a particular case, it may be cited and relied upon in subsequent cases with similar facts or legal issues.

3. **Guidance for Legal Arguments**:
   - Lawyers and litigants often cite relevant case law to support their legal arguments, positions, and interpretations of the law.
   - Case law provides guidance and authority for advancing legal theories, advocating for specific outcomes, and persuading courts to adopt particular interpretations.

4. **Resolution of Disputes**:
   - Courts use case law to resolve disputes, apply legal principles, and render judgments in civil, criminal, and administrative cases.
   - Judges analyze precedents, distinguish relevant facts, and apply legal reasoning to reach decisions consistent with established legal principles.

5. **Development of Legal Doctrine**:
   - Case law contributes to the development and evolution of legal doctrine, principles, and jurisprudence over time.
   - Courts may adapt, refine, or expand legal doctrines based on changing societal norms, technological advancements, and emerging legal challenges reflected in case law.

[12/04/24, 11:56:09â€¯AM] Abdul Shaikh: import java.net.*;

public class server {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        try (DatagramSocket socket = new DatagramSocket(1200)) {
            byte[] receiveData = new byte[4096];
            System.out.println("Server is running.....");
            while (true) {
                DatagramPacket receivePacket = new DatagramPacket(receiveData, receiveData.length);

                socket.receive(receivePacket);

                String request = new String(receivePacket.getData(), 0, receivePacket.getLength());

                if (request.equalsIgnoreCase("q")) {
                    System.out.println("Server shut down");
                    System.exit(0);

                } else {

                    String result = processRequest(request);
                    InetAddress clientAddress = receivePacket.getAddress();
                    int clientPort = receivePacket.getPort();
                    DatagramPacket sendPacket = new DatagramPacket(result.getBytes(), result.length(),
                            clientAddress, clientPort);
                    socket.send(sendPacket);
                }
            }
        } catch (Exception e) {
            e.printStackTrace();
        }
    }

    private static String processRequest(String request) {
        // Implement your logic to process the request and return the result
        // For simplicity, let's assume the request is in the format "operation value1 value2"
        String[] parts = request.split(" ");
        String operation = parts[0];
        int value1 = Integer.parseInt(parts[1]);
        int value2 = Integer.parseInt(parts[2]);

        switch (operation.toLowerCase()) {
            case "add":
                return String.valueOf(value1 + value2);
            case "sub":
                return String.valueOf(value1 - value2);
            case "mul":
                return String.valueOf(value1 * value2);
            case "div":
                return String.valueOf(value1 / value2);
            case "q":
                return "Shutdown";
            default:
                return "Invalid operation";
        }
    }
}

import java.net.DatagramSocket;
import java.net.InetAddress;
import java.util.Scanner;

public class client {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        try (
                DatagramSocket socket = new DatagramSocket())
        {
            InetAddress serverAddress = InetAddress.getByName("192.168.0.104"); // Replace with the server's IP address

            Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
            // Example request: "add 10 5"
            String request = sc.nextLine();

            byte[] sendData = request.getBytes();
            DatagramPacket sendPacket = new DatagramPacket(sendData, sendData.length, serverAddress, 1200);
            socket.send(sendPacket);

            // Receive the result
            byte[] receiveData = new byte[4096];
            DatagramPacket receivePacket = new DatagramPacket(receiveData, receiveData.length);
            socket.receive(receivePacket);
            System.out.println(receivePacket);

//            String result = new String(receivePacket.getData(), 0, receivePacket.getLength());
//            System.out.println("Result: " + result);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            e.getMessage();
        }
    }
}
